# Chapter 1: Items System

## Overview

The VEIN items system encompasses all physical objects that players can interact with, collect, and use in the game. Items are primarily implemented as Blueprints (BP_) and are organized into several major categories.

## Item Categories

## Property Schemas

Common properties found in item blueprints:


## Modding Guide

### Creating a New Item

1. Choose an existing item as a template
2. Copy the JSON file
3. Rename the asset (update NameMap entries)
4. Modify properties as needed:
   - Display name
   - Description
   - Weight
   - Stack size
   - Icon reference
5. Convert back to .uasset
6. Pack into mod

### Key Properties to Modify

- **DisplayName**: Item name shown to player
- **Description**: Item description text
- **Weight**: Item weight (affects inventory)
- **MaxStackSize**: How many can stack in one slot
- **IconPath**: Reference to item icon texture
- **BaseDurability**: Item condition/durability
- **BaseValue**: Monetary value

### Testing Your Item

1. Add item to a spawn list or give command
2. Test in-game pickup and usage
3. Verify icon displays correctly
4. Check stats and effects work as intended
